                    <div class="row">
                        <div class="nv-single-page-wrap col">
                            <div class="nv-content-wrap entry-content">
                                <div class="wp-block-cover alignfull">
                                    <span aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-cover__background has-background-dim-10 has-background-dim" style="background-color:#526d83"></span>
                                    <img decoding="async" width="720" height="254" class="wp-block-cover__image-background wp-image-330" alt="" src="https://vit.edu/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/Rectangle-93-4_cleanup-1.webp" data-object-fit="cover" srcset="https://www.vit.edu/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/Rectangle-93-4_cleanup-1.webp 720w, https://www.vit.edu/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/Rectangle-93-4_cleanup-1-300x106.webp 300w" sizes="(max-width: 720px) 100vw, 720px"/>
                                    <div class="wp-block-cover__inner-container is-layout-flow wp-block-cover-is-layout-flow">
                                        <p class="has-text-align-left about-page banner-text has-nv-site-bg-color has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-baa1f6ea03112905573a00214c9e9c93" style="padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--80);padding-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--80);font-size:49px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">
                                            Over 40 years of<br>Educational Excellence
                                        </p>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <h1 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-left has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-73f2986e6f52cf89e4741dfff99d49fb" id="0-the-birth-of-a-legend" style="color:#333333;padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">The Birth of a Legend</h1>
                                <div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-44 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
                                    <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:80%">
                                        <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-615be2478747d29765da62aeec080c8d" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">In the 1980s, there were very few engineering colleges in Maharashtra. Quality engineering education was not accessible to all. During this time, our founder, Shri Rajkumarjee Agarwal, came in touch with two like-minded educational officers, Shri V.V. Chiplunkar Sir and Shri Sarnobat Sir and the idea of Vishwakarma Institute of Technology was born. The name Vishwakarma was inspired by the eponymous divine engineer from Indian mythology, who is known to have engineered the world.
</p>
                                        <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-21f4d18f33b51ac555f7cd446874434d" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">
                                            <br>Driven by the vision of quality education for all, VIT, Pune, was launched on 1 September 1983. The institute started operations from a small building &#8211;Shri Mangal building in a busy marketplace of Pune. The theory classes were held in a school nearby, New English School. The institute was even ridiculed by the newspaper for such an arrangement. But the institute moved to its current Bibwewadi Campus in 1987, and the rest, as they say, is history. In 2008, VIT, Pune, became the first private, self-financed autonomous engineering college in Maharashtra state.
                                        </p>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="wp-block-column is-vertically-aligned-top has-background is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="background-color:#f3f3f3;padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);flex-basis:24%">
                                        <figure class="wp-block-image size-full is-resized">
                                            <img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="179" height="135" src="https://www.vit.edu/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/Vector.webp" alt="" class="wp-image-361" style="width:146px;height:auto"/>
                                        </figure>
                                        <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-ad2bd5416f97d9d0ef7a71d7392d901a" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">
                                            <em>
                                                First they ignore you,<br>
                                                then they laugh at you,<br>
                                                then they fight you,<br>then you win.”
                                            </em>
                                        </p>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div style="height:30px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
                                <hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity is-style-default"/>
                                <div style="height:30px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
                                <div class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-block wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-pills wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-holder vertical-holder wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-horizontal-holder-mobile wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-vertical-holder-tablet" id="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469">
                                    <div class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-holder vertical-tab-width horizontal-tab-width-mobile vertical-tab-width-tablet">
                                        <div role="tablist" class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tabs-title-vertical-tab wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tabs-title-mobile-horizontal-tab wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tabs-title-tablet-vertical-tab">
                                            <div role="tab" id="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-tab-0" aria-controls="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-panel-0" aria-selected="false" class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-vertical-wrap wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-tablet-vertical-wrap" tabindex="-1">
                                                <div class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title">Institute</div>
                                            </div>
                                            <div role="tab" id="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-tab-1" aria-controls="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-panel-1" aria-selected="false" class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-vertical-wrap wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-tablet-vertical-wrap" tabindex="-1">
                                                <div class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title">Trust</div>
                                            </div>
                                            <div role="tab" id="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-tab-2" aria-controls="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-panel-2" aria-selected="false" class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-vertical-wrap wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-tablet-vertical-wrap" tabindex="-1">
                                                <div class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title">Leadership</div>
                                            </div>
                                            <div role="tab" id="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-tab-3" aria-controls="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-panel-3" aria-selected="true" class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-vertical-wrap wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-tablet-vertical-wrap active" tabindex="-1">
                                                <div class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title">Deans</div>
                                            </div>
                                            <div role="tab" id="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-tab-4" aria-controls="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-panel-4" aria-selected="false" class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-vertical-wrap wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-tablet-vertical-wrap" tabindex="-1">
                                                <div class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title">Registrar Office</div>
                                            </div>
                                            <div role="tab" id="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-tab-5" aria-controls="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-panel-5" aria-selected="false" class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-vertical-wrap wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-tablet-vertical-wrap" tabindex="-1">
                                                <div class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title">
                                                    Online Transcript<br>Application
                                                </div>
                                            </div>
                                            <div role="tab" id="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-tab-6" aria-controls="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-panel-6" aria-selected="false" class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-vertical-wrap wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-tablet-vertical-wrap" tabindex="-1">
                                                <div class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title">Examination Office</div>
                                            </div>
                                            <div role="tab" id="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-tab-7" aria-controls="ub-tabbed-content-ac6a9fa1-f132-4a7b-bb46-0bfad668a469-panel-7" aria-selected="false" class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-vertical-wrap wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title-tablet-vertical-wrap" tabindex="-1">
                                                <div class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-title">Committees</div>
                                            </div>

                                    <div class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tabs-content vertical-content-width  vertical-content-width-tablet">
                                        <div role="tabpanel" class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-content-wrap ub-hide" id="ub-tabbed-content--panel-0" aria-labelledby="ub-tabbed-content--tab-0" tabindex="0">
                                            <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-479e8ad90811ab72cdd7e29c68f7b904" id="9-vit-pune" style="color:#333333;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">VIT, Pune</h2>
                                            <div style="height:15px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
                                            <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-683e0bdbbcfa9b35f889b6e125e6367d" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">Vishwakarma Institute of Technology, Pune, is an autonomous institute permanently affiliated with the Savitribai Phule Pune University. The Institute was granted autonomous status in AY 2008-09, valid until 2030. The Institute ranks among the premier technical institutes in the western region of India.</p>
                                            <div class="wp-block-columns bulb_pad is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-45 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
                                                <div class="wp-block-column is-vertically-aligned-top has-background is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="background-color:#f3f3f3;padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);flex-basis:33.33%">
                                                    <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-010d181be38dfd63971048e97149547f" id="10-vision" style="color:#333333;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">Vision</h2>
                                                    <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-ceeabca0cb35fa33d75125eaa4b5b5dc" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">To be a globally acclaimed Institute in Technical Education and Research for holistic socio-economic development.</p>
                                                </div>
                                                <div class="wp-block-column is-vertically-aligned-stretch has-nv-site-bg-color has-text-color has-background has-link-color wp-elements-207576114c69ce7b92f00dc0a599b7be is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="background-color:#10203f;padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);flex-basis:66.66%">
                                                    <h2 class="wp-block-heading" id="11-mission" style="font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">Mission</h2>
                                                    <ul class="wp-block-list">
                                                        <li style="font-style:normal;font-weight:400">To ensure that 100% of students are employable and employed in industry, higher studies, entrepreneurship, civil or defence services, government jobs, and other areas like sports and arts.</li>
                                                        <li style="font-style:normal;font-weight:400">To strengthen Academic Practices in Curriculum, Pedagogy, Assessment and Faculty Competence.</li>
                                                        <li style="font-style:normal;font-weight:400">To Promote Research Culture among Students and Faculty through Projects and Consultancy</li>
                                                        <li style="font-style:normal;font-weight:400">To make students Socially Responsible Citizens</li>
                                                    </ul>
                                                </div>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-53 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
                                                <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
                                                    <div class="wp-block-columns has-background is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-49 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex" style="background-color:#ebf9ff">
                                                        <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:30%">
                                                            <div class="wp-block-image">
                                                                <figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized">
                                                                    <img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="256" height="256" src="https://www.vit.edu/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/Bulb-1.webp" alt="" class="wp-image-411" style="width:342px" srcset="https://www.vit.edu/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/Bulb-1.webp 256w, https://www.vit.edu/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/Bulb-1-150x150.webp 150w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 256px) 100vw, 256px"/>
                                                                </figure>
                                                            </div>
                                                        </div>
                                                        <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:80%">
                                                            <div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-48 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
                                                                <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:45%">
                                                                    <div class="wp-block-group course-offered-no is-layout-flex wp-block-group-is-layout-flex" style="padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50)">
                                                                        <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-77afb4a2d4eca1aec38a179d57635fbd" style="color:#003294;font-size:55px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">9</p>
                                                                        <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-842feef18e6aa0e58a9028ce6b8b73ab" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-size:25px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">
                                                                            UG Courses<br>Offered
                                                                        </p>
                                                                    </div>
                                                                    <div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-46 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
                                                                        <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="padding-top:0;padding-bottom:0">
                                                                            <div class="wp-block-group course-offered-no is-layout-flex wp-block-group-is-layout-flex" style="padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50)">
                                                                                <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-aff4e6e3f833b176a19ce4a632fd73b2" style="color:#003294;font-size:55px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">3</p>
                                                                                <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-6acd00b052154985e73fc5c22697b912" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-size:25px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">
                                                                                    PhD Courses<br>Offered
                                                                                </p>
                                                                            </div>
                                                                        </div>
                                                                    </div>
                                                                </div>
                                                                <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:65%">
                                                                    <div class="wp-block-group course-offered-no is-layout-flex wp-block-group-is-layout-flex" style="padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50)">
                                                                        <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-9d56ba44de1f306ce2de758af451cbb6" style="color:#003294;font-size:55px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">3</p>
                                                                        <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-d77edd8258bbc708a3a472c6dd96b41d" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-size:25px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">
                                                                            PG Courses<br>Offered
                                                                        </p>
                                                                    </div>
                                                                    <div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-47 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
                                                                        <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
                                                                            <div class="wp-block-group course-offered-no bulb_pad is-layout-flex wp-block-group-is-layout-flex" style="padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50)">
                                                                                <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-69fe5b1bc42bece046aa5c25071cf35b" style="color:#003294;font-size:54px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">1200</p>
                                                                                <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-b774338f9ee7a504b961250ba3c86509" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-size:25px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">
                                                                                    Yearly Student <br>Intake
                                                                                </p>
                                                                            </div>

                                                    <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-474dd7d48c2a6ede0b80c40feb1c3505" style="color:#333333;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">Technical Education Quality Improvement Programme by Ministry of HRD, New Delhi.</p>

                                            <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-51d4a7bfe1ea673b6e365e845fa55cca" id="1-bansilal-ramnath-agarwal-charitable-trust-bract" style="color:#333333;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">Bansilal Ramnath Agarwal Charitable Trust (BRACT)</h2>
                                            <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
                                            <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-0d3b30c42c089a4ad5673ec61821de70" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">Vishwakarma Institute of Technology, Pune, is run by the Bansilal Ramnath Agarwal Charitable Trust (BRACT). The Trust was established on 16 June 1975 under the Bombay Trust Act of 1950. The Trust undertakes social, religious and educational activities to nurture talent, innovation and creativity.

</p>
                                            <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-14a9961c68e6e8aa60045e8661dcc58f" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">Technical and Management Institutes started by BRACT</p>
                                            <ul style="color:#003294;font-style:normal;font-weight:700" class="wp-block-list has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-95fb70f12079d151640d2e6cb5e7ea20">
                                                <li>Vishwakarma Institute of Technology, Pune</li>
                                                <li>Vishwakarma Institute of Information Technology, Pune</li>
                                                <li>Vishwakarma Junior College of Arts, Commerce, Science, Pune</li>
                                                <li>Vishwakarma College of Arts, Commerce, Science, Pune</li>
                                                <li>Suman Ramesh Tulsiani Charitable Trust &#8217;s &#8211;Suman Ramesh Tulsiani Technical Campus, at Kamshet, Tal. Maval, Dist. Pune</li>
                                                <li>Sandipani Technical and Medical Education Institute &#8217;s Sandipani Technical Campus &#8211;Faculty of Engineering, Latur</li>
                                                <li>Dnyanshree Institute of Engineering &amp;Technology, Sajjangad Road, Satara</li>
                                                <li>Prakash Shikshan Prasarak Mandal &#8217;s Manajiraje Bhosale Technical Campus &#8211;Faculty of Engineering, Islampur &#8211;Sangli Road, Urun Islampur, Tal. Walwa, Dist. Sangli</li>
                                            </ul>
                                            <div class="wp-block-columns has-background is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-54 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex" style="background-color:#ebf9ff">

                                                    <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-a6cc890d46f806cfb5961a4559484188" style="color:#333333;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">List of Trustees</h2>

                                                    <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-f12c2c072add084f533e75b1625b97f1" id="3-chairman" style="color:#333333;font-style:normal;font-weight:400;text-transform:uppercase">Chairman</h2>
                                                    <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-63c1ccc7f0891cde8de414efc26b28b3" id="4-shri-rajkumarji-agarwal" style="color:#003294;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">Shri Rajkumarji Agarwal</h2>
                                                    <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-096d9d20a7dc99354b54afb49cf14fcd" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">“Vishwakarma Institute of Technology, Pune, was established in 1983 to create highly competent engineers. The institute aims to make its students technologically advanced by providing the necessary infrastructure, cooperative networking, and excellent placements to keep them updated with the latest industry trends.”</p>

                                                    <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-d246d804f66d168eab971614aa299ed2" id="5-managing-trustee" style="color:#333333;font-style:normal;font-weight:400;text-transform:uppercase">Managing Trustee</h2>
                                                    <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-ae3fe80066d7d4bfe52865c1aae871e0" id="6-bharat-agarwal" style="color:#003294;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">Bharat Agarwal</h2>
                                                    <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-893b3b95a210782c768fe02bd690bc59" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">“At the Vishwakarma Institute of Technology, Pune, we are dedicated to offering our students numerous opportunities to enhance their talent and skills. Our goal remains constant and unwavering: to train engineers to become responsible professionals and citizens in a highly competitive global environment.”</p>

                                                    <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-d4460ad6592c44a9ea444295a938acf8" id="7-director" style="color:#333333;font-style:normal;font-weight:400;text-transform:uppercase">Director</h2>
                                                    <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-cdb8f38a1d8a12d557888eb57539b682" id="8-prof-dr-r-m-jalnekar" style="color:#003294;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">Prof. Dr. R. M. Jalnekar</h2>
                                                    <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-81f0b45e394dcfb7372964fc25dc79d2" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">The Bansilal Ramnath Agarwal Charitable Trust founded the Vishwakarma Institute of Technology in 1983. Over four decades, the Institute has expanded both in terms of its breadth and depth. It currently provides University of Pune-accredited undergraduate, postgraduate, and doctoral programmes across various disciplines, including mechanical engineering, computer engineering, E &amp;TC, chemical engineering, instrumentation, and industrial engineering.</p>
                                                    <div class="wp-block-ub-expand ub-expand" id="ub-expand-2e977422-07b9-4244-89ba-e8d6432cc8e7" data-scroll-type="fixedamount" data-scroll-amount="200">
                                                        <div class="ub-expand-portion ub-expand-partial" id="ub-expand-portion-3f5a0b80-5ed7-4927-9b3e-788b4227ae0e">
                                                            <a class="ub-expand-toggle-button" role="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ub-expand-full-882d5fb5-06a0-4233-8ba2-c58419a16d52" tabindex="0">Read more</a>
                                                        </div>
                                                        <div class="ub-expand-portion ub-expand-full ub-hide" id="ub-expand-portion-899961e9-9440-42e7-b7e0-9ac84c1d1ad8">
                                                            <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-b6fc3785381c6d34aad76e6a0a8e7a80" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">The Institute achieved a significant milestone in its development when the University Grants Commission and the University of Pune granted it Academic Autonomy. As a result, the Institute can create its curriculum and academic calendar, administer exams and announce results. The Institute &#8217;s primary goal is to nurture entrepreneurs with the skills and integrity to contribute to the technical and socio-economic advancement of the nation. To achieve this, the Institute has incorporated Honors/Minor Streams, General Proficiency Courses, Professional Development Courses, Skill Development Courses, Semester Projects, Open Electives (such as Psychology, Sociology, Philosophy, Economics, etc.), and Soft Skills into its curriculum. Additionally, the Institute offers various facilities such as fast-track courses, course dropping, registration for extra credits, and Industrial training. Students can also benefit from summer internships and semester internships in Industry. As part of its curriculum update, the Institute is currently working on incorporating Digital Technology (DT) to enhance the learning experience.</p>
                                                            <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-685e81c3ecabf0898e2b302fe5098bb5" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">The Institute has established academic collaborations, collaborative research, student exchange, and Global Internship programmes with several esteemed foreign universities such as Binghamton University in the USA, Nanyang Technological University in Singapore, Purdue University in the USA, Hof University in Germany, a group of 17 universities from the State of Ontario in Canada, Group des Ecoles des Mines in France, and the Asian Institute of Technology based in Bangkok. More than 15 students from all branches benefit from this unique international exposure each year. In March 2016, 104 students went to NTU in Singapore for around four weeks for the Global Internship Program. These initiatives provide a valuable platform for faculty and students of Vishwakarma Institute of Technology in Pune to engage in synergistic interaction with faculty and students from these universities, bringing immense value to our student community. We aim to implement more student-centric systems in the future.</p>
                                                            <a class="ub-expand-toggle-button" role="button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="ub-expand-full-882d5fb5-06a0-4233-8ba2-c58419a16d52" tabindex="0">Read less</a>
                                                        </div>
                                                    </div>
                                                </div>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>

                                                    <ul style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400" class="wp-block-list has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-260aadf3a2fdbd2b4a59d057f53c775d">

                                                    <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-44c628aa6e260d9a1e5b4ea9854a3439" style="color:#333333;font-size:24px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">Establishment Section</h2>
                                                    <ul style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400" class="wp-block-list has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-9a7b2660a1c410320eaa63760fce0617">

                                                            Minutes of the Meetings

                                                            <ul class="wp-block-list">

                                                            </ul>
                                                        </li>
                                                        <li>Strategic Plan</li>
                                                    </ul>

                                            <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-1877b448f9c16893c521824e6d231fcd" style="color:#333333;font-size:24px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">Faculty Recruitment</h2>
                                            <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
                                            <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-25caf1265c177ad27723c8cf44e9dfde" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:600">Faculty recruitment procedure is as per the AICTE norms, which are given below:</p>
                                            <ul style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400" class="wp-block-list has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-ca71354f845753d600c6f8cf7b9b058f">
                                                <li>Faculty for Undergraduate programs is as per the staff: Student Ratio, i.e. 1:15, and cadre ratio is 1:2:6 (1 Professor, 2 Associate Professors, 6 Assistant Professors)</li>
                                                <li>Faculty for Postgraduate programs is as per the staff: Student Ratio, i.e. 1:1, and cadre ratio is 1:1 (1 Professor 1 Associate Professor)</li>
                                                <li>Send your applications only to careers@vit.edu</li>
                                            </ul>
                                            <div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-76 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
                                                <div class="wp-block-column has-background is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="background-color:#ebf9ff;padding-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50);padding-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--50)">
                                                    <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-01f0acfcb8a86e37c76a571adb1bc59c" style="color:#333333;font-size:24px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">Accounts Section</h2>
                                                    <div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
                                                    <div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-75 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">

                                                            <p class="has-text-color has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-2f6609f44525353eca75ed793754973e" style="color:#a6a6a6">(Accounts Officer)</p>
                                                            <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-4d66a7dc3928fe67c73506e978144b85" style="color:#003294;font-style:normal;font-weight:600;text-transform:uppercase">Profile: Centralised Finance &amp;Accounts Unit</p>
                                                            <div style="height:15px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
                                                            <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-21cfa478d594ee0be77793d8a0cc082a" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">

                                                            </p>

                                                                <img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="27" height="27" class="wp-image-504" style="width: 27px;" src="https://www.vit.edu/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/call.webp" alt="">(020)24202290
                                                            </p>
                                                        </div>

                                                    <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-c7519a205f0e0d8db13125a9c8775438" style="color:#2257bf;font-size:15px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">

                                                            Fees proposal to FRA for the year 2023-24 <img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="14" height="14" class="wp-image-490" style="width: 14px;" src="https://betawp.vit.edu/wp-content/uploads/2024/03/Group-148334.webp" alt="">
                                                        </a>
                                                    </p>
                                                    <ul style="color:#4d4d4d;padding-right:var(--wp--preset--spacing--80);padding-left:var(--wp--preset--spacing--80);font-style:normal;font-weight:400" class="wp-block-list has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-3e69597613096141c4d49257f31f467c">
                                                        <li>Income and Expenditure</li>
                                                        <li>Institute Information</li>
                                                        <li>Faculty Details</li>
                                                    </ul>
                                                    <p></p>
                                                    <ul style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400" class="wp-block-list has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-b46706f86fc5b250e4afd18f19e71816">
                                                        <li>Collection of tuition fees, development, examination fees, university fees, hostel fees, deposit etc</li>
                                                        <li>Fees will be refunded as per the rule of the Director of Technical Education (DTE) &amp;in case of admission cancellation, refund to year down (YD) students</li>
                                                        <li>Refund/payment of necessary scholarships, freeships, education loans, earn &amp;learn, students stipend &amp;other refunds required as per norms</li>
                                                        <li>Issue various fee structures to the students for educational loan purposes. Various letters/certificates for education loans to the bank. Coordination with local banks &amp;Credila Company</li>
                                                        <li>&nbsp;Maintenance of fees register</li>
                                                        <li>Online fee collection system through the payment gateway Examination work of University and autonomous</li>
                                                    </ul>
                                                    <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-d5266cc6160335027b740ebb71f05e26" style="color:#333333;font-size:17px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">ACCOUNTS</p>
                                                    <ul style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400" class="wp-block-list has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-f0f896b8b086abc1b52907fd764bd183">
                                                        <li>Budget preparation &amp;distribution to departments</li>
                                                        <li>Account finalisation Receipt &amp;payments, Income &amp;expenditure &amp;audited financial reports. Budget analysis</li>
                                                        <li>Account updation &amp;verification</li>
                                                        <li>Stock verification</li>
                                                    </ul>
                                                    <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-5c3da569cf8018eb6aa52a83f6c7607c" style="color:#333333;font-size:17px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">STAFF SECTION</p>
                                                    <ul style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400" class="wp-block-list has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-0fb88a310cc85c10fd318fe1c336a8a6">
                                                        <li>Salary for teaching and non-teaching staff, including taxation (TDS) work, Income Tax declaration scrutiny and TDS return work, Distribution of salary slips through mail and issue of form 16 to employee and form 16 A to contractor &amp;professional consultant</li>
                                                        <li>Provident Fund, Profession Tax, Income Tax, Gratuity etc. arrears work</li>
                                                        <li>Employees welfare, insurance &amp;Medical policy Karmachari Patsanstha work</li>
                                                        <li>Necessary advances &amp;bills settlement</li>
                                                        <li>Day-to-day petty cash transactions</li>
                                                        <li>All bank reconciliations, proposals, project reports, etc</li>
                                                        <li>Internal &amp;statutory audit &amp;compliance report</li>
                                                        <li>Compliance to FEES REGULATING AUTHORITY, AICTE, DTE, SPPU and banks</li>
                                                    </ul>
                                                </div>

                                        <div role="tabpanel" class="wp-block-ub-tabbed-content-tab-content-wrap ub-hide" id="ub-tabbed-content--panel-5" aria-labelledby="ub-tabbed-content--tab-5" tabindex="0">
                                            <p class="d-none">
                                                <a href="https://betawp.vit.edu/online-transcript-application/" data-type="page" data-id="779">Go To Online Transcript Application</a>
                                            </p>
                                            <div style="height:0px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
                                            <div class="wp-block-group">
                                                <div class="wp-block-group__inner-container is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained">
                                                    <div class="wp-block-group">
                                                        <div class="wp-block-group__inner-container is-layout-constrained wp-block-group-is-layout-constrained">
                                                            <h1 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-1a92e0a9b30e14ab7af1595210ea48d1" style="color:#333333;font-size:28px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">Online Transcript Application</h1>
                                                            <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-8147b4ea9dc2764eeafa462c40bcccd3" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">You can now apply and send transcripts online.</p>
                                                            <ul style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400" class="wp-block-list has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-fe54206492f9a3ac0adf6f994bafe725">
                                                                <li>Create and submit your transcript for approval online</li>
                                                                <li>&nbsp;When you upload your transcript for approval, you will be directed to a payment gateway for online payment. There is a fee of ₹1050/- for getting your transcript approved</li>
                                                                <li>Upon payment, your document will be forwarded for review</li>
                                                                <li>After approval of your transcript from the Institute (which may take 2-3 days), you will receive an email with a stamped PDF version of your approved transcript</li>
                                                                <li>You can use the PDF to upload your online application to US universities</li>
                                                                <li>The approved PDF will also be retained on the VIT, Pune server for future use if required by the student</li>
                                                            </ul>
                                                            <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-d5fac6c8d0032537f3f0edadb9e840cc" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">If you need to send official transcripts to universities, you have two options:</p>
                                                            <ul style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400" class="wp-block-list has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-003bdf10dc19820f7cc79d2da229d03b">
                                                                <li>
                                                                    eTranscripts: VIT can send eTranscripts to most universities in the US via the electronic Transcript network. <mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-primary-color">(Click Here) </mark>
                                                                    . To send eTranscripts, you can apply online, specifying the recipient university, and the eTranscript will go directly from VIT, Pune. You will receive an acknowledgement of delivery in an email. The charge for this service is ₹800 per destination
                                                                </li>
                                                                <li>Paper Transcripts: You can request stamped and sealed paper transcripts. These can be picked up from the Institute, or they can be couriered to any address. Paper transcripts are sent to US Universities via DHL; you will receive the DHL number for online tracking. Printing, handling and courier charges can be paid online for this service</li>
                                                            </ul>
                                                            <p class="has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-b2d70c427863668c6891f667bb87b66a" style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400">&nbsp;How To Apply Online</p>
                                                            <ul style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400" class="wp-block-list has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-07e57498769efcd85fa3e6412813b814">
                                                                <li>Download the appropriate transcript template for your course/department and edit the template to create your transcript. Please follow all instructions on that page to create your transcript from the template</li>
                                                                <li>Fill in your information, and upload a single PDF of your mark sheet scans when applying for the transcript</li>
                                                            </ul>
                                                            <div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-77 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
                                                                <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:49%">
                                                                    <p class="has-text-align-left has-text-color has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-fcd348f60040db14346eefef5fd084ee" style="color:#2257bf;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">
                                                                        <a href="https://files.truecopy.in/vit/vit_landing.html" data-type="link" data-id="https://files.truecopy.in/vit/vit_landing.html" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Download the template</a>
                                                                    </p>
                                                                </div>
                                                                <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:70%">
                                                                    <p class="has-text-align-left has-text-color has-link-color has-medium-font-size wp-elements-8c1eb51a2ed76e258d7b0f9ac433c8b6" style="color:#2257bf;font-style:normal;font-weight:700">
                                                                        <a href="https://vit.truecopy.in/v2/files/submitdoctranscript.tc" data-type="link" data-id="https://vit.truecopy.in/v2/files/submitdoctranscript.tc" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Apply Online</a>
                                                                    </p>
                                                                </div>
                                                            </div>
                                                        </div>
                                                    </div>

                                            <div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-79 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
                                                <div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:70%">
                                                    <div class="wp-block-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-78 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
                                                        <div class="wp-block-column is-vertically-aligned-stretch is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow" style="flex-basis:30%">

                                            <h2 class="wp-block-heading has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-98ba2b9dc49cece60ddee2dfd0ca5c4f" style="color:#333333;font-size:24px;font-style:normal;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">Roles of Exam Section</h2>
                                            <ul style="color:#4d4d4d;font-style:normal;font-weight:400" class="wp-block-list has-text-color has-link-color wp-elements-44ccfb45f9acc4e8eac8ce21a07bd89b">
                                                <li>Exam conduction for UG and PG programmes</li>
                                                <li>Result processing and Result declaration of UG, PG programmes</li>
                                                <li>Issuing marksheets and conversion certificates</li>
                                                <li>Issuing various certificates like rank certificate, attempt certificate, other certificates on request</li>
                                                <li>The issuing Duplicate Certificates/Mark Sheets on request</li>
                                                <li>Preparation of Gazette and submission to SPPU</li>
                                                <li>Facilitating Revaluation Processes</li>
                                            </ul>
                                            <div class="wp-block-columns has-text-color has-background has-link-color wp-elements-fbdf82ef8885ba6404caacb8d9a38979 is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-80 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex" style="color:#ebf9ff;background-color:#ebf9ff">

        <script>
            // Get the button
            let mybutton = document.getElementById("myBtn");

            // When the user scrolls down 20px from the top of the document, show the button
            window.onscroll = function() {
                scrollFunction()
            }
            ;

            function scrollFunction() {
                if (document.body.scrollTop > 20 || document.documentElement.scrollTop > 20) {
                    mybutton.style.display = "block";
                } else {
                    mybutton.style.display = "none";
                }
            }

            // When the user clicks on the button, scroll to the top of the document
            function topFunction() {
                document.body.scrollTop = 0;
                document.documentElement.scrollTop = 0;
            }
        </script>

        <script>

            $(document).ready(function() {
                var theLetters = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ";
                //You can customize what letters it will cycle through
                var ctnt = "AAAA";
                // Your text goes here
                var speed = 100;
                // ms per frame
                var increment = 8;
                // frames per step. Must be >2

                var clen = ctnt.length;
                var si = 0;
                var stri = 0;
                var block = "";
                var fixed = "";
                //Call self x times, whole function wrapped in setTimeout
                (function rustle(i) {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        if (--i) {
                            rustle(i);
                        }
                        nextFrame(i);
                        si = si + 1;
                    }, speed);
                }
                )(clen * increment + 1);
                function nextFrame(pos) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < clen - stri; i++) {
                        //Random number
                        var num = Math.floor(theLetters.length * Math.random());
                        //Get random letter
                        var letter = theLetters.charAt(num);
                        block = block + letter;
                    }
                    if (si == (increment - 1)) {
                        stri++;
                    }
                    if (si == increment) {
                        // Add a letter; 
                        // every speed*10 ms
                        fixed = fixed + ctnt.charAt(stri - 1);
                        si = 0;
                    }
                    $(".counterchar").html(fixed + block);
                    block = "";
                }
            });
        </script>

        <script id="neve-script-js-after">
            var html = document.documentElement;
            var theme = html.getAttribute('data-neve-theme') || 'light';
            var variants = {
                "logo": {
                    "light": {
                        "src": "https:\/\/www.vit.edu\/wp-content\/uploads\/2024\/09\/Group-148284.webp",
                        "srcset": "https:\/\/www.vit.edu\/wp-content\/uploads\/2024\/09\/Group-148284.webp 543w, https:\/\/www.vit.edu\/wp-content\/uploads\/2024\/09\/Group-148284-300x76.webp 300w",
                        "sizes": "(max-width: 543px) 100vw, 543px"
                    },
                    "dark": {
                        "src": "https:\/\/www.vit.edu\/wp-content\/uploads\/2024\/09\/Group-148284.webp",
                        "srcset": "https:\/\/www.vit.edu\/wp-content\/uploads\/2024\/09\/Group-148284.webp 543w, https:\/\/www.vit.edu\/wp-content\/uploads\/2024\/09\/Group-148284-300x76.webp 300w",
                        "sizes": "(max-width: 543px) 100vw, 543px"
                    },
                    "same": true
                }
            };

            function setCurrentTheme(theme) {
                var pictures = document.getElementsByClassName('neve-site-logo');
                for (var i = 0; i < pictures.length; i++) {
                    var picture = pictures.item(i);
                    if (!picture) {
                        continue;
                    }
                    ;var fileExt = picture.src.slice((Math.max(0, picture.src.lastIndexOf(".")) || Infinity) + 1);
                    if (fileExt === 'svg') {
                        picture.removeAttribute('width');
                        picture.removeAttribute('height');
                        picture.style = 'width: var(--maxwidth)';
                    }
                    var compId = picture.getAttribute('data-variant');
                    if (compId && variants[compId]) {
                        var isConditional = variants[compId]['same'];
                        if (theme === 'light' || isConditional || variants[compId]['dark']['src'] === false) {
                            picture.src = variants[compId]['light']['src'];
                            picture.srcset = variants[compId]['light']['srcset'] || '';
                            picture.sizes = variants[compId]['light']['sizes'];
                            continue;
                        }
                        ;picture.src = variants[compId]['dark']['src'];
                        picture.srcset = variants[compId]['dark']['srcset'] || '';
                        picture.sizes = variants[compId]['dark']['sizes'];
                    }
                    ;
                }
                ;
            }
            ;
            var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
                mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
                    if (mutation.type == 'attributes') {
                        theme = html.getAttribute('data-neve-theme');
                        setCurrentTheme(theme);
                    }
                    ;
                });
            }
            );

            observer.observe(html, {
                attributes: true
            });
            function toggleAriaClick() {
                function toggleAriaExpanded(toggle='true') {
                    document.querySelectorAll('button.navbar-toggle').forEach(function(el) {
                        if (el.classList.contains('caret-wrap')) {
                            return;
                        }
                        el.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true' === el.getAttribute('aria-expanded') ? 'false' : toggle);
                    });
                }
                toggleAriaExpanded();
                if (document.body.hasAttribute('data-ftrap-listener')) {
                    return;
                }
                document.body.setAttribute('data-ftrap-listener', 'true');
                document.addEventListener('ftrap-end', function() {
                    toggleAriaExpanded('false');
                });
            }
            var menuCarets = document.querySelectorAll(".nav-ul li > .wrap > .caret");
            menuCarets.forEach(function(e) {
                e.addEventListener("keydown", e => {
                    13 === e.keyCode && (e.target.parentElement.classList.toggle("active"),
                    e.target.getAttribute("aria-pressed") && e.target.setAttribute("aria-pressed", "true" === e.target.getAttribute("aria-pressed") ? "false" : "true"))
                }
                ),
                e.parentElement.parentElement.addEventListener("focusout", t => {
                    !e.parentElement.parentElement.contains(t.relatedTarget) && (e.parentElement.classList.remove("active"),
                    e.setAttribute("aria-pressed", "false"))
                }
                )
            });
            function initNoLinkDD() {
                var noLinkDDs = document.querySelectorAll('.header-menu-sidebar-inner .menu-item-has-children a[href="#"]');

                if (noLinkDDs.length < 1) {
                    return;
                }

                noLinkDDs.forEach(function(noLinkDD) {
                    var dropdownButton = noLinkDD.parentElement.querySelector('button');
                    noLinkDD.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                        e.preventDefault();
                        dropdownButton.click();
                    });
                });
            }
            window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', initNoLinkDD);
        </script>

            var popoverTriggerList = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('[data-bs-toggle="popover"]'));
            var popoverList = popoverTriggerList.map(function(popoverTriggerEl) {
                return new bootstrap.Popover(popoverTriggerEl)
            });
            var tooltipTriggerList = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('[data-bs-toggle="tooltip"]'));
            var tooltipList = tooltipTriggerList.map(function(tooltipTriggerEl) {
                return new bootstrap.Tooltip(tooltipTriggerEl)
            });
            var modals = document.getElementsByClassName("modal");
            var modal_links = [];
            for (var i = 0; i < modals.length; i++) {
                var modal = modals.item(i);
                var links = document.querySelectorAll("[href=\'#" + modal.id + "\']");
                if (!links.length) {
                    continue
                }
                for (var modal_i = 0; modal_i < links.length; modal_i++) {
                    modal_links.push(links.item(modal_i))
                }
            }
            if (modal_links.length) {
                modal_links.forEach(function(link) {
                    link.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                        event.preventDefault();
                        var id = link.href.split("#");
                        var modal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById(id[1]),{
                            keyboard: false
                        });
                        modal.show()
                    }, false)
                })
            }
            var collapses = document.getElementsByClassName("collapse");
            var collapse_links = [];
            for (var i = 0; i < collapses.length; i++) {
                var collapse = collapses.item(i);
                var links = document.querySelectorAll("[href=\'#" + collapse.id + "\']");
                if (!links.length) {
                    continue
                }
                for (var link_i = 0; link_i < links.length; link_i++) {
                    collapse_links.push(links.item(link_i))
                }
            }
            if (collapse_links.length) {
                collapse_links.forEach(function(link) {
                    link.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                        event.preventDefault();
                        var id = link.href.split("#");
                        var collapse = new bootstrap.Collapse(document.getElementById(id[1]),{
                            keyboard: false
                        });
                        collapse.toggle()
                    }, false)
                })
            }
            var offcanvass = document.getElementsByClassName("offcanvas");
            var offcanvas_links = [];
            for (var i = 0; i < offcanvass.length; i++) {
                var offcanvas = offcanvass.item(i);
                var links = document.querySelectorAll("[href=\'#" + offcanvas.id + "\']");
                if (!links.length) {
                    continue
                }
                for (var link_i = 0; link_i < links.length; link_i++) {
                    offcanvas_links.push(links.item(link_i))
                }
            }
            if (offcanvas_links.length) {
                offcanvas_links.forEach(function(link) {
                    link.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                        event.preventDefault();
                        var id = link.href.split("#");
                        var offcanvas = new bootstrap.Offcanvas(document.getElementById(id[1]),{
                            keyboard: false
                        });
                        offcanvas.show()
                    }, false)
                })
            }
            var toasts = document.getElementsByClassName("toast");
            var toast_links = [];
            for (var i = 0; i < toasts.length; i++) {
                var toast = toasts.item(i);
                var links = document.querySelectorAll("[href=\'#" + toast.id + "\']");
                if (!links.length) {
                    continue
                }
                for (var link_i = 0; link_i < links.length; link_i++) {
                    toast_links.push(links.item(link_i))
                }
            }
            if (toast_links.length) {
                toast_links.forEach(function(link) {
                    link.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
                        event.preventDefault();
                        var id = link.href.split("#");
                        var toast = new bootstrap.Toast(document.getElementById(id[1]),{
                            keyboard: false,
                        });
                        toast.show()
                    }, false)
                })
            }
            jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
                $('.areoi-tabs').each(function() {
                    var active = $(this).find('.nav a.active:first-of-type');
                    $(this).find('.nav a.active:not(:first-of-type)').removeClass('active');
                    $(this).find('> div').addClass('tab-pane d-none');
                    var active_tab = $(this).find(active.attr('href'));
                    if (active_tab) {
                        active_tab.removeClass('d-none')
                    }
                });
                $(document).on('click', '.areoi-tabs .nav a', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    var container = $(this).parents('.areoi-tabs');
                    var active_tab = container.find($(this).attr('href'));
                    container.find('.nav a').removeClass('active');
                    $(this).addClass('active');
                    if (active_tab) {
                        container.find('> div').addClass('d-none');
                        active_tab.removeClass('d-none')
                    }
                })
            });
        </script>
